[30;1m27 | [0m[35mclass TimeSeriesDataFrame(pd.DataFrame):[0m
[30;1m28 | [0m[35m    """A collection of univariate time series, where each row is identified by an (``item_id``, ``ti[0m
[30;1m29 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m30 | [0m[35m    For example, a time series data frame could represent the daily sales of a collection of product[0m
